Shanghai Business Community Cables Requesting Careful Negotiations with Japan. The Four Northeastern Provinces are Chinese Territory. The National People Do Not Want to Abandon Them. Why Does the Agreement with Japan on Traffic, etc., Preserve Our Homeland and Bind the Hearts of the People? 113

City Chamber of Commerce Cables 114

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce cabled the National Government yesterday, stating: "To the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the Nanjing National Government: Negotiations with Japan have created doubts and caused damage. The people of the whole country are feeling anxious. We recently read Premier Wang's report to the Legislative Yuan stating that our side has decided not to sacrifice sovereignty as a principle. After reading this, we felt extremely gratified. The Four Northeastern Provinces are Chinese territory, this is a major matter of sovereignty. The people will never be willing to abandon them under any circumstances. In the past, during the European War, the entire territory of Belgium was devastated, but they never yielded and eventually recovered their original territory. Moreover, the League of Nations resolution and the sympathy of friendly nations provide guarantees. How can we abandon it ourselves? We earnestly request that the central government consistently adhere to the principle of not harming sovereignty, thereby fulfilling the expectations of the whole country and avoiding unforeseen outcomes. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce bows respectfully."

Shipping Association Cables 115

The Shanghai Shipping Trade Association sent a telegram yesterday, saying: "To Premier Wang of the Nanjing Executive Yuan, President Sun of the Legislative Yuan, and Chairman Jiang of Nanchang: We have recently seen reports that our country is directly negotiating with Japan on transportation, postal services, and customs in the Northeast. If this is true, it is tantamount to recognizing the puppet state and forfeiting the Four Provinces. If the Four Provinces can be forfeited, it is tantamount to wasting all the sacrifices of the people over the past two years. How can we protect the country and bind the hearts of the people? Negotiations between China and Japan are extremely difficult. But no matter what, we dare to ask you to devise other appropriate measures to cope with the situation, so as to comfort the spirit of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and fulfill the hopes of the people. We boldly offer our opinion, and we hope you will consider and accept it. Yu Hede, Chairman of the Shanghai Shipping Trade Association, respectfully bows."

Cotton Industry Control Committee Announces the Process of Stabilizing the Yarn Market. Banks in China and Shanghai Advance Funds. Organization of He Xing Company to Purchase and Stock Yarn. All Measures are to Rescue the Cotton Industry. 116

The New News reporter recently visited the officials of the Cotton Industry Control Committee after the Shanghai Yarn and Cloth Exchange resumed operations after its suspension. They asked the officials about the truth of the committee's stabilization of yarn prices. The person in charge explained in detail: "Since the establishment of the committee under orders to control the cotton industry, the basic and temporary solutions have been carefully discussed before being implemented step by step. Recently, in view of the sluggish yarn sales, which is the biggest pain for manufacturers, it is necessary to make adjustments. Over the past two weeks, we have dealt with the matter fairly, with the sole purpose of maintaining the yarn industry and taking into account the interests of the majority of the people. We have heard rumors, which are not credible. Here is a detailed account of what happened":

Reasons for Stabilizing Cotton Yarn Prices 117

At the beginning of its establishment, this association received an official letter from the Ministry of Finance, which stated that the Taxation Administration had reported that, according to the United Association of Chinese Cotton Mills, the recent decline in cotton mill business was mainly due to the excessive amount of cotton yarn stored in the Cotton Yarn Exchange, which had led to a sharp drop in yarn prices. They proposed that the government should invest funds to purchase 30,000 bales of cotton yarn stored in the exchange to slightly increase yarn prices and maintain the cotton industry. It was confirmed that the recent decline in yarn prices was a fact. If no measures were taken to provide relief, it was feared that the prices would continue to fall, further affecting the only important domestic enterprise. As your committee has been organized and established, we hereby forward the letter to your association, hoping that you will promptly investigate the actual reasons for the drop in yarn prices and discuss relief measures within a possible scope to maintain the cotton industry. This association, upon receiving the letter, held several meetings of the Standing Committee. It was generally agreed that although there were multiple reasons for the drop in yarn prices, the massive amount of cotton yarn stored in the exchange was the crux of the matter. Therefore, it was resolved that this association should urge manufacturers to organize a company to purchase the stored yarn as much as possible and distribute it to various regions for sales, as a fundamental solution. This is the method adopted by this association to facilitate the clearance of stored yarn.

Organizing a Company for Bank Loans 118

To purchase the stored yarn, a suitable company was required. Therefore, this association invited enthusiastic manufacturers to form the He Xing Company, which would serve as the organization for purchasing the stored yarn. This association was well aware that this stored yarn was of low quality and had to be sold at reduced prices, which would inevitably result in significant losses in the future. This association has already sent a letter to the government requesting subsidies to offset the losses. Since the middle of last month, purchases have been made successively. By the end of last month, He Xing Company had purchased a total of 21,150 pieces of yarn. The final settlement for the month required a net amount of 4,073,067 yuan. This association negotiated with six banks, including China, Shanghai Commercial & Savings, Continental, Zhejiang Industrial, National Goods, and Women's Bank, as well as three money shops, including Yongfeng, Hengxun, and Fuyuan, to provide loans on a pro rata basis.

Deciding on Three Rectification Measures 119

Our country's exchange receives cotton yarn based on trademarks, not on quality standards. This allows manufacturers to take advantage of the opportunity to produce low-quality cotton yarn specifically for delivery to the exchange, further providing speculators with opportunities for dumping. This association has repeatedly discussed and decided on the following measures: (1) Notify the Cotton Mill Association to inform all factories to strictly abide by the resolution of the association on July 8, that no cotton yarn will be delivered to the exchange from that date until the end of this year. (2) Notify the Cotton Yarn Exchange that, starting from October, all delivered cotton yarn shall be subject to quality inspection by personnel dispatched by this association to prevent inferior yarn from entering the exchange. (3) Work with the exchange to revise cotton standards and inspection regulations to provide a basis for compliance.

The Course of the Exchange Suspension 120

Of the cotton yarn purchased by He Xing Company, apart from the majority being yarn stored in the exchange's warehouses, 7,200 pieces were found to be newly delivered goods by the seller, which was inconsistent with the resolution of the Cotton Mill Association on July 8. This association, considering that the resolution of the meeting had not been implemented and that there was a lack of good faith, and that the new standards would not be implemented until six months later, while the current standard yarn was of low quality and its validity period was only two months, requested the Ministry of Industry to instruct the exchange to refuse to receive newly delivered cotton yarn from November to the end of December. After receiving the order, the exchange immediately announced its implementation. However, the brokers became concerned and stopped trading. The exchange had no choice but to announce a three-day suspension of trading from the 6th of this month.

All Measures to Rescue the Cotton Industry 121

This association believes that the actions of the exchange's brokers were due to a misunderstanding of the intentions of the Ministry of Industry and this association. Since the purpose of He Xing Company's purchase of goods is to stabilize yarn prices, the cotton yarn purchased is mainly intended for distribution to various ports. Even if the market price rises excessively, before the stock purchased by He Xing Company is sold out, this association can still order it to be released in appropriate quantities for regulation. To protect the business of the exchange, this association is willing to provide sincere assistance to the various rectifications of the exchange. Now that the exchange has also understood this intention and has resumed cotton yarn trading, with prices returning to stability, this association expresses its satisfaction. In summary, the Ministry of Industry and this association, for the sake of stabilizing cotton yarn market prices, have taken all measures to rescue the cotton industry from its crisis, which is beneficial to the yarn market. Those who are insightful will share this view.

The Railway Bureau Has Established Regulations for Employees to Ride Through Trains. It Is Required to Have Special and Urgent Official Business. Yesterday, an Order Was Issued to All Departments to Comply With. 127

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration has recently established temporary regulations for employees to ride through trains for special and urgent official business. Yesterday, a special order was issued to all departments to comply with. The order and regulations are recorded below.

Order to All Departments 128

It has been found that all long-term travel permits and official travel certificates issued by this bureau cannot be applied to Shanghai-Pinglian through trains according to the Ministry's order. An order has been issued to all departments to comply with it. However, there are occasional cases where special and urgent official business cannot be handled without riding the Shanghai-Pinglian through train. It is necessary to formulate alternative measures to facilitate official business. Now, five regulations for employees of both railways to ride through trains for special and urgent official business have been formulated and promulgated. In addition to distributing them, they should be complied with and communicated to the subordinates to comply with them. This order,

Provisional Measures 129

(1) Employees of both railways may ride Shanghai-Pinglian through trains in accordance with the provisions of these measures for the following special and urgent official business: (A) In the event of an accident on a train or station, it is necessary to rush to rescue. (B) The route is blocked, and it is necessary to rush to repair it. (C) Responsible for other special and urgent tasks. (2) When employees of both railways ride Shanghai-Pinglian through trains for special and urgent official business, they should first pay the fare in advance and purchase a ticket to ride the train. Afterwards, they should submit a request for approval to reimburse the fare. (3) Those who have no money to pay temporarily may have the supervisor sign a certificate and temporarily record the account with the station master to collect the ticket. All payable fares will be transferred to the traffic department by the head of each competent department or office after the approval is issued, and submitted to the accounting department for settlement. (4) Regardless of whether the ticket is purchased with advanced payment or the ticket is collected on credit, the reason, date, departure and arrival station names, ticket price, and ticket number should be listed in detail and reported for review afterwards. Those who report falsely will be subject to appropriate punishment in addition to the personal responsibility for the ticket price. (5) These measures will be implemented after being reviewed and approved by the director. If there are any omissions, the director will amend them at any time.

The Naval Jiangfeng No. 1 Aircraft Was Completed and Test Flown Yesterday Morning. The Takeoff Was Temporarily Suspended Due to Insufficient Tire Pressure. The Date of the Return to the Factory for Reassembly and the Flight to the South Is Undecided.

Zeng Yijing, the director of the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Office, in order to complete the national flight plan, replaced the pontoons of the self-made Jiangfeng aircraft with land wheels to fly to South China. The work was completed yesterday and a test flight was conducted. However, the land wheels leaked air, and the aircraft was returned for reassembly. The details are as follows:

Completing the Plan 130

The Aircraft Manufacturing Office was ordered to awaken the public, promote aviation to save the country, and recognize China's self-made aircraft. The Jiangfeng aircraft was flown westward along the Yangtze River from Shanghai. After returning to Shanghai, it was invited by the Nantong Chamber of Commerce to fly to Nantong to negotiate the purchase of self-made aircraft. Now, in order to prepare to fly to South China and complete the national flight plan, the pontoons of the Jiangfeng aircraft were replaced with land wheels. The work was completed the day before yesterday. Yesterday, a test flight was conducted at the Hongqiao Airport. It is planned to depart from Shanghai within this week, passing through Hangzhou, Ningbo, Wenzhou, Fuzhou, and arriving at Xiamen, and then fly to the South at a later date.

Completed and Test Flight 131

At 9:00 AM yesterday, the Jiangfeng aircraft was transported from the Gao Miao Aircraft Manufacturing Office to the Hongqiao Airport. Director Zeng Yijing, engineers Ma Deshu and Wang Chonghong, and others went to the airport in advance to make arrangements. The Jiangfeng aircraft was escorted by pilot Xu Chengqi. It arrived at the airport at 10:30 AM. Xu Chengqi piloted the aircraft and took off at 11:30 AM. When it was taxiing on the ground preparing for takeoff, it was temporarily suspended because the land wheels leaked air.

Return to the Factory 132

After inspection by engineers Wang Chonghong and others, it was found that the air pressure in the land wheels was insufficient and needed to be reinstalled. However, since the parts were all in the manufacturing office, the Jiangfeng aircraft was transported back to the manufacturing office at 1:00 PM to be repaired. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency met Director Zeng last night. According to him, the reassembly of the land wheels on the Jiangfeng aircraft will be completed soon. As for the date of the flight to South China, it will be determined after the work is completed.

Sixth Day of the Bandit Suppression Propaganda Week. Yesterday Afternoon, a Motorcade Paraded in Nanshi. Mayor Wu Broadcast a Speech Yesterday. 133

The city's bandit suppression propaganda campaign entered its sixth day yesterday, which was Motorcade Day. More than 80 vehicles and 50 bicycles participated in the motorcade. The route was originally planned to start from Heping Road in Ximen, pass through the concessions, and end in the city center. However, as a result of the negotiations between the city party headquarters and the authorities of the Public Concession and the French Concession, it was believed that at a time when the Communist Party was lurking in the concessions, it might cause trouble. The motorcade was not allowed to pass through. Therefore, the standing committee meeting of the city party headquarters yesterday decided that the motorcade route would start from Heping Road in Ximen, circle the city, and end at Heping Road again. Several large oil painting banners were hung on the cars, and party flags and large white cloth banners were inserted and hung on each car. The Public Security Bureau sent a military band to liven things up, and there were also eight patrol cars to maintain order. Mayor Wu also broadcast a speech for the Bandit Suppression Propaganda Week, entitled "The Bandit Suppression Work and the Prosperity of Shanghai." His speech is as follows:

Serious Significance This city is holding a bandit suppression propaganda week today. As the head of this city, I would like to use the topic "The Bandit Suppression Work and the Prosperity of Shanghai" to explain the serious significance of the bandit suppression work, so that all citizens can deeply understand the tragic nature of the bandit disaster in China today, rise up together, support this serious and arduous work, and jointly eliminate this bandit scourge that harms the people and the country.

Scorched Earth Policy Since the Chinese Communist Party decided on its "scorched earth policy" at the so-called "August 7" meeting (emergency meeting on August 7, 1927), the people in the bandit areas have been living under the lewd power of the Red Bandits and groaning in the depths of the water and fire for six years. Except for a few scholars and scholars who live comfortably in the city, live comfortably, and watch the fire from the other side, they are still chewing their pens and sucking their ink, talking and arguing, and criticizing the bandit suppression, almost all citizens who have a little blood and a little responsibility deeply hate the tragic nature of the bandit disaster and earnestly hope that the Red Disaster will be eliminated as soon as possible.

Unprecedented According to a telegram from Chairman Chiang, the bandit areas in the three provinces of Henan, Anhui, and Hubei are all like poor borderlands, and everything has been swept away. There are no houses that have not been burned, no trees that have not been felled, no chickens and dogs that have been left behind, and no cattle that have not been killed. Only the cries of the wild are heard, and no smoke from the cooking fires can be seen. In some cases, thousands or even tens of thousands of people prostrate themselves before the army, with emaciated faces and bodies, and lie stiffly on the left side of the road. The tragedy is unprecedented. According to the statistics of the bandit areas investigated by the General Headquarters for Bandit Suppression in the border areas of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, only Shangcheng County, with a population of 350,000, has been captured by bandits, and only two-fifths of the county's area has been affected. The number of people killed has reached 10,000, and the number of refugees has reached 107,000. The total number of refugees and people killed accounts for half of the total population. 343,000 houses have been burned down, 150,000 heads of livestock have been lost, and the loss of property can be estimated at 10 million yuan. The area of ​​farmland that has been abandoned accounts for more than six-tenths of the county's area. According to the statistics of Shangcheng County alone, the losses are so alarming. If we combine the statistics of all the bandit areas, the losses and disasters to the nation, the country, the society, and the economy are beyond calculation. If this disaster is not eliminated and this scourge is not eradicated, how can the country stand and how can the people survive?

The Disease Is in the Abdomen Examining the history and studying the reasons for order and disorder, it is inevitable that a great chaos will follow a famine. At a time when bandit disasters are rampant and disasters are coming together, and dangerous situations are emerging one after another, all Chinese people, if they do not rise up together to eliminate this scourge that harms the country and the people, will inevitably suffer the great disaster of the entire people being overthrown. On July 30 this year, Premier Wang and Chairman Chiang sent a telegram to inform the people of the country, saying that the way to save the country today is to enrich the national strength, and the way to treat the symptoms is to clear the Communist bandits. If the national strength is not strong, it is because the people's strength is not sufficient. If the people's strength is not sufficient, it is because the rural areas are bankrupt and the industry is immature. Therefore, the business is invisibly declining. If we give up the development of the national productivity, there is no other way to enrich the national strength. The bandits are rampant, and the disease is in the abdomen. The red flames are full of the world, and people are reduced to animals. If they are not suppressed, not only will the people have no peace and happiness to speak of, but all plans will be constrained, and even defending the country and resisting foreign aggression will not be effectively implemented. The Central Committee is concerned about this, so it has concentrated its troops and carefully suppressed the bandits in order to clear the bandit disaster in the shortest possible time and eliminate the greatest hidden danger to this nation and country.

Closely Related Although Shanghai is the richest area in the country, its prosperity is also based on the internal security of the country. I have often said that Shanghai is like a fish and the inland is like water. In recent years, although the population and wealth of Shanghai have increased greatly, and there seems to be a trend of development and prosperity, the communist bandits in the inland provinces have caused rural bankruptcy, and wealthy families have flocked to Shanghai with their money and property to seek security, while the farmers who are struggling to make a living have also come here to solve their livelihood problems.

However, it is not known that the concentration of wealth without knowing how to circulate it is not a sign of urban prosperity. The increase in population and the increasing number of unemployed people is a pathological condition of urban life. It is impossible to expect a fish to grow without first filling the pond with water. Therefore, today's bandit suppression work, although it is directly aimed at seeking the safety of the people in the inland and the recovery of the rural economy, is indirectly aimed at promoting the development and prosperity of Shanghai. The inland and Shanghai are not only closely related like lips and teeth, but also like fish and water. Therefore, the citizens of Shanghai, although living in this rich and happy environment, should think more about the suffering of the inland people and the hardships of being displaced. At a time when we are actively suppressing the communist bandits, we should unite and do our best to help the progress of the bandit suppression work.

Beware of Disregard Alas, the tragic disasters of the late Ming Dynasty are not far away. Thinking of danger in times of peace, beware of disregard. A spark can set a prairie fire, and a bandit disaster can destroy a country. I urge all citizens to rise up together and swear to eliminate this hidden danger to the nation's heart and abdomen in order to save this nation from the great disaster of destruction.

The text of the document is as follows: "It has been found that the city's taxes have been owed for many years. Orders have been issued repeatedly to urge the collection of taxes. It is necessary to issue a strict order to the tax collection police chief to instruct all tax collection police officers to comply with the order and clear all taxes owed up to the 20th year of the Republic by the end of November this year. As for the 28th, 29th, and 30th guarantees, the situation is special, and each should pay at least 10,000 yuan within the deadline. Those who can comply with the order and clear the taxes owed after the deadline will be awarded a month's salary to encourage them. Japan's Foreign Trade Exports 30 Million Yuan More Than Imports Japanese Are Very Satisfied 136

The Japanese Commercial Counselor's Office received an official telegram from Tokyo yesterday. In October of this year, the total value of Japanese exports was 170 million Japanese yen, exceeding the total value of imports by 30 million Japanese yen. All major exports, except for raw silk, are satisfactory. As for imports, cotton, wool, iron, and kerosene are all large amounts. Therefore, the total foreign trade for the ten months of this year is still in deficit by 38 million Japanese yen. However, the deficit has decreased by 42% compared to the same period last year. Also, when the foreign trade of Japan and its colonies is combined, the deficit for the nine months of this year is also 38 million Japanese yen, which is a decrease of 27% compared to the deficit for the same period last year. Also, in September of this year, Japanese exports to China were worth 11.3 million Japanese yen, exceeding imports by 1.5 million Japanese yen. The total surplus for the nine months of this year is 21 million Japanese yen, but the surplus has decreased by 65% compared to the same period last year. If we divide it by region, Japanese exports to South China decreased by 55% in September, exports to North China decreased by 26%, exports to Central China decreased by 4%, and exports to Hong Kong increased by 1%. As for the amount of Japanese imports to Central China and South China, the value is also very large.

Change of Japanese Fleet 24th and 26th 137

Yesterday's Shanghai Japanese newspaper stated that the four ships of the 24th Destroyer Squadron, which were dispatched to the Yangtze River in October of the year before last, have now returned to Shanghai and are moored at the Osaka Merchant Marine Wharf in Yangshupu. The commander of the squadron, Lieutenant Commander Sakano, the captain of the Momo Destroyer Squadron, Lieutenant Commander Tachibana, the captain of the Tso ship, Lieutenant Commander Haneda, and the captain of the Yanagi ship, Lieutenant Commander Yanagawa, are preparing to leave Shanghai at 8:00 AM today (the 12th) and return to their home port of Sasebo to be replaced by the 26th Squadron.

Jianghai Public Notice Loading Trucks Sealed by Customs Implemented Starting January 1 Next Year 141

The Customs Commissioner of Jianghai issued a public notice yesterday, stating, "It has been found that loading trucks are used to load goods from the docks to private and public warehouses far from the waterways, or to transport goods that have not paid taxes from the warehouses. Starting from January 1, 1934, the truck body must be properly fitted for sealing by this customs. It is not allowed to open it privately along the way. All truck merchants are expected to comply with this."

Pudong Dongjiadu Rickshaw Pullers Strike Yesterday Morning. Police Station Orders Police to Suppress, No Disturbances Occur. Party Headquarters Dispatches Personnel to Thoroughly Investigate the Cause of the Strike. 142

Dagon Society reports that there are over 320 rickshaw pullers in Dongjiadu, Pudong. These pullers rent vehicles from rickshaw companies daily, and after paying the rental fee, they rely on the remaining earnings to make a living. Because these pullers have no specific employer to address, disputes have never occurred. Unexpectedly, starting at 7:00 AM yesterday, dozens of pullers suddenly parked their rickshaws in vacant lots and declared a strike. However, some who had not joined the strike continued to pull their rickshaws. These striking members then blocked them along the way and ordered them to join. By a little after 8:00 AM, all 300+ rickshaws were at a standstill. A Dagon Society reporter inquired with the pullers about the reason for the strike, but all responded that they did not know. However, according to another source, it was said to be due to incitement by reactionary elements.

Dispatch Police to Suppress 143

Zhang Mingqin, the Third District Chief of the Public Security Bureau, reported that rickshaw pullers in Dongjiadu had suddenly gone on strike and were blocking passengers along the way. Fearing disturbances, he immediately dispatched an inspector with more than twenty armed police officers to suppress the strike. After the police persuaded the pullers, order was restored, and no disturbances occurred. However, the pullers continued to strike into the evening.

Party Headquarters Thorough Investigation 144

The Municipal Party Headquarters, upon hearing that rickshaw pullers in Dongjiadu had suddenly declared a strike, and mindful of the covert and active presence of the Communist Party, feared that unscrupulous elements were inciting the workers. Therefore, in addition to telegraphing the Public Security Bureau to dispatch police to maintain order, it also ordered the Civil Affairs Department to send personnel across the Huangpu River to thoroughly investigate the truth in order to take appropriate action.

Tianzhang Paper Mill Workers in Yangshupu Road Stage Work Stoppage Yesterday Morning, Opposing the Factory's Dismissal of Workers 145

The West Factory of Tianzhang Paper Mill on Dalianwan Road, Yangshupu Road, employs over one hundred male and female workers. Recently, the company, citing poor business, reduced wages, calculating them at 80%, causing dissatisfaction among all workers. They petitioned the Party and government for mediation, which has not yet been resolved. Unexpectedly, the company suddenly dismissed more than thirty workers the day before yesterday, causing extreme indignation among all the workers. Starting at 8:30 AM yesterday morning, they unanimously staged a work stoppage. The factory immediately expelled the workers from the factory, and the situation was quite serious. It is reported that all the workers are scheduled to petition the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Social Bureau, and the General Labor Union on Monday, requesting assistance.

Telephone Bureau Notifies Users to Reduce the Number of Calls 152

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications issued a notice to users yesterday, stating: "To whom it may concern: Since the integration of Chinese and foreign call charges into the monthly rental, the daily number of calls has increased from 4,000 to 12,000, causing abnormal congestion on the bureau's lines and heavy workload for the traffic bureau. We are currently trying to expand our capacity, but all mechanical equipment must be ordered from abroad, which will take about three months. During this time, due to line limitations, new user installation requests cannot be processed immediately. The bureau is therefore incurring losses and additional subsidies, but to facilitate users, we should temporarily endure the pain. However, we hope that valued users will, to the extent possible, reduce the number of calls as much as possible, so that public convenience can be taken into account. We have always admired your enthusiasm and care, and we are making a suggestion. Please take it to heart. We are sincerely grateful. Sincerely, the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications."

In ancient Chinese etiquette, there was a provision against killing without reason. In modern times, foreign countries have associations prohibiting mistreatment. Although it may not be possible to immediately stop killing, it is still possible to reduce it. This is well known to all gentlemen. In the past, Ms. Lü Bicheng compiled "The Light of Europe and America," which included an article on the origins of creating an animal protection association, marking the beginning of the animal protection movement in China. The cause of planting cruelty is the cause of creating the disaster of war. Therefore, whether or not world wars can be eliminated depends not on international agreements, but on the compassion and violence in people's hearts. Overcoming cruelty and eliminating killing cannot be achieved by chance. This is why the progress of this association cannot be delayed. We believe that everyone's love of goodness is no less than our own, and the cause of protecting life deserves more help. Moreover, this association aims for great unity and does not involve any religious prejudices or any status claims. Participants are widely recruited from all walks of life to participate together, to widely solicit comrades, to generously join, or to widely persuade, or to establish branches to facilitate implementation and promote benevolence. Rental Dispute in Taoyuanfang Resolved 158

In Taoyuanfang, located at the intersection of North Henan Road, Qipu Road, and North Jiangxi Road, a dispute arose over rent increases, lasting for several months without any resolution. The landlord, Yongkang Company, suddenly filed a lawsuit in court against several households. The main members of the tenant union in the neighborhood, Kong Rixuan, He Xiaodong, Qian Changcui, Zhao Yaoting, Xu Muxian, Xu Xi, Feng Biao, etc., tried their best to cope, and the situation almost escalated. Fortunately, Mr. Feng Bingnan, a Chinese director of the Public Works Department, came forward to mediate and agreed on a compromise as follows: (1) Rent will be increased from July 1, 1933, according to the following standards: (Original rent) 20 yuan, (compromise) add 3.5 yuan; 33 yuan add 4.5 yuan; 43 yuan add 5.5 yuan; 30 yuan add 4 yuan; 37 yuan add 5 yuan; 68 yuan add 8.5 yuan. (2) Iron gates will be installed at all alley entrances within 1933, and gatekeepers will be added. (3) The landlord will be responsible for repairing damaged houses immediately. (4) Sanitation and cleaning within the alleys will be improved. The rattan workers and various vendors, which were vehemently opposed by all tenants in previous general meetings and were extremely unbearable, must be completely cleared by the landlord within one week. Both parties have fully accepted and exchanged written evidence. The rent increase turmoil has come to a peaceful end.

Jiande Bank Establishes Hongkou Branch 160

Since moving into the new premises at Tianhougong Bridge, the Jiande Bank in this city has seen its business flourish, with deposits and savings increasing daily. In order to expand its business, it has established a branch under the Zhonghong Bridge in Hongkou to meet the needs of Hongkou residents. It has also hired Li Rongqi, a veteran in the financial industry, as the branch manager, and Sun Yuandou, a wealthy businessman from Nanjing, as the assistant manager. The bank has strong capital and thorough equipment. It is recently heard that, in order to give preferential treatment to depositors, the bank will build more than a hundred affordable housing units on over ten acres of land in Qiujiang Road owned by the assistant manager, Mr. Shen, and rent them to depositors at half price, in order to revitalize the market in the North Bin district. The purity and nobility of its intentions are commendable. It is heard that the branch is scheduled to officially open on the 15th. It is expected that there will be a grand occasion at that time.

Over a Hundred Thatched Sheds Reduced to Ashes at the North Gate Outside Great Western Road Bridge: A Scene Reminiscent of the Devastating Fire Last Winter; A Child's Private Baking of Cakes Turns into a Major Disaster; Hundreds Left Homeless in a Pitiful State 161

The area around Great Western Road Bridge, in the Tanziwan area north of the Gate, has long been occupied by a group of poor people from Jiangbei, whose thatched sheds stand in rows, forming a market town. Those traveling to and from Beijing and Hangzhou can see them from the train windows when passing by the Great Western Road Bridge station. Last winter, a fire broke out in the thatched sheds south of the Great Western Road Bridge, burning everything to the ground. The tragic scene at that time saddened those who witnessed it. Unexpectedly, at 2:00 PM yesterday, just as the various fire brigades were extinguishing a fire at the Yuan Da Oil Press on Hengfeng Road, the thatched sheds north of the Great Western Road Bridge suddenly burst into flames, creating a scene no less tragic than that of the previous year. The cause of the fire was that a man from Jiangbei named Yu Jinbao had built a thatched shed north of the Great Western Road Bridge as his residence and set up a cake stall in front of it. Yesterday afternoon around 2:00 PM, Yu Jinbao had to go out, leaving only his son, who was just over ten years old, at home. The child, being playful, saw that his father was not there and secretly made cakes from flour and roasted them over the fire, hoping to satisfy his hunger. Before long, he completely forgot about it and went outside to play with the neighboring children. However, the fire in the cake oven was burning fiercely, and there was no fire cover on top, so it heated the straw and, combined with the dry weather of late and the intense heat, it ignited instantly. White smoke billowed, and flames blazed. When neighbors discovered it, it was already too late. People scattered in all directions, and the surrounding houses caught fire simultaneously. Moreover, straw is a highly flammable material, so in a moment, everything was engulfed in flames. The sound of weeping and wailing shook the heavens. People, old and young, fled for their lives, unable to escape in time. Upon hearing the alarm, the fourth district and third police stations of the Tanziwan area immediately dispatched police to maintain order. At the same time, they urgently telegraphed the various fire brigades in Zhabei to rush to the scene to put out the fire. However, the situation was already beyond control. The flames rose high, and the red light filled the sky, leaving the firefighters with no place to start. They tried their best to protect the other houses that had not been affected, while pulling down the burning thatched sheds and pouring water around them. But the fire kept flaring up here and there until around 5:00 PM, when it was finally completely extinguished. However, more than 110 thatched sheds and 21 tile-roofed houses along the north bank had already been reduced to ashes. A group of poor people, looking emaciated, sat on the ground south of the bridge, gazing at the disaster area, tears streaming down their faces. In addition, the weather was cold, and they had lost their shelter, so they were all shivering and pitiful. The young and old were begging for food, awaiting charity from philanthropists. Yu Jinbao and his son, who had caused the disaster, were apprehended by the police from the fourth district and third police station after the incident and escorted to the fourth district headquarters for questioning. That evening, the district arranged for rice and porridge to be cooked and distributed to the victims. Fortunately, there were no deaths or injuries. At the same time, the China Water & Electric Co. plant near the fire scene was also spared, which can be considered very fortunate, otherwise, the consequences would have been even more unimaginable.

$5,000 Robbery Case: Shen Qixiang Robbed While Delivering Money; All Banknotes Had Secret Marks 162

Qiu Yuru, the owner of the Juxing Qianzhuang (money exchange) at Yuqi Bridge in the Public Concession, established a Nanshi office inside Yuan Da Pig Shop in Yong'an Lane, Sixteenth Ward, last spring to facilitate deposits and withdrawals for Nanshi customers. Yesterday at around 11:00 AM, Zhang Qianqian, the director of the office, suddenly received calls from Yuan Yu Rice Shop on Wanyu Wharf inside Limalu and Yongli Flower Shop on Laiyi Wharf inside Limalu, requesting funds. He then handed 5,000 yuan in banknotes to an apprentice, Shen Qixiang, to deliver to the respective establishments. Among this money, 3,000 yuan consisted of five-yuan banknotes from the Bank of China, each marked with the character "濤" (Tao) in all four corners. The remaining 2,000 yuan consisted of five-yuan banknotes from the China Industrial Bank, each marked with the character "天" (Tian) in all four corners. The apprentice wrapped the banknotes in old newspaper and carried them under his left shoulder. He walked out of the office, hired a rickshaw, and intended to deliver 3,000 yuan to Yuan Yu Rice Shop first and 2,000 yuan to Yongli Flower Shop. Unexpectedly, as he was passing the entrance to Jiuhe Lane on Guanqiao Inside Limalu, two robbers suddenly appeared. One was wearing a blue cloth short-sleeved shirt and pants, and the other was wearing a black short-sleeved shirt and pants. They ran up from behind Shen's rickshaw, stopped the vehicle, and each pulled out a pistol, ordering Shen not to make a sound. The robber wearing black clothes reached out and forcibly snatched the bundle of 5,000 yuan from Shen, carrying the loot and fleeing north. The robber wearing blue clothes, seeing that the money had been obtained, ordered the rickshaw puller to move forward. After a few steps, he turned around and fled south. At this time, Shen, regaining his composure, jumped off the rickshaw and shouted for help to catch the robbers. Qin Fan, the guard at the Twelfth Post, heard the commotion and rushed to pursue, but because the area was crowded with people, the two robbers disappeared into the crowd in an instant, failing to be apprehended. The incident was immediately reported to the First District Headquarters. Currently, District Chief Guan Gong is ordering a strict investigation.

Nephew Extorts Aunt: Tong Lianzhong Bored and Destitute; Tong Xie Clan Reports to the Authorities and Case Solved 163

Yongli Dyeing Factory, located at No. 2, Lane 97, Puyu East Road, outside the Great South Gate of Nanshi, had a thriving business, attracting the attention of bandits. In June of this year, a group of thugs broke into the factory and shot and killed Tong Baoshun, the factory owner, before fleeing without a trace. Tong's wife, Xie, reported the incident to the police, who opened a case for investigation. However, since Tong's death, Xie has been managing the factory. Unexpectedly, on the second of this month, she received a threatening letter. The letter stated that due to a large number of brothers and the difficulty of making a living, the author was requesting a loan of 5,000 yuan. She was asked to prepare the money, wrap it in red paper, and send someone to wait inside the China Garden outside the Great Western Road Bridge in the Public Concession from 3:00 PM to 5:00 PM on the tenth, where someone would come to make contact. If she did not comply with the letter, there would be consequences. The letter was signed "Wang Tongren." At the time, Xie believed it was just a letter of extortion, so she ignored it. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the seventh, she received another threatening letter of the same kind. She immediately reported the incident to the Third Precinct of the First District, who then forwarded it to the First District Headquarters. District Chief Guan Gong dispatched detectives to coordinate with the Chinese and foreign detectives of the Public Concession Police.

Proposal to Reduce Rent 164

Wang Xingyi, a standing committee member of the China National Products Preservation Association, proposed that since the bankruptcy of rural areas, people have little wealth, their homes are bare, and general purchasing power has weakened, which has affected all industries and businesses, leading to their decline. The various industries in Shanghai have also suffered as a result. This is evidenced by the "Great Sale" and "Great Sacrifice" banners flying on various roads year-round. However, rents in Shanghai have always been high, and at a time of commercial decline, not only have they not decreased, but they have continued to increase, causing business operators to sigh that their income is insufficient to cover the rent. As a result, those with some assets are afraid of doing business and dare not venture into it, leading to newly built commercial buildings remaining empty and unoccupied for long periods of time. In view of this, Wang Xingyi, a standing committee member of the China National Products Preservation Association, proposed that the association initiate a request to the Municipal Social Bureau to convene various important organizations to form a Rent Evaluation Committee to find ways to reduce rents, thereby alleviating social panic and maintaining industrial and commercial livelihoods. This matter concerns the prosperity and decline of Shanghai and is of great importance. It is hoped that all sages will work together to assist and urge its implementation, so that it can be realized. This would not only be fortunate for Shanghai but also for the entire country. The full text of his proposal is excerpted below: (Proposal) In order to alleviate the decline of all industries and businesses in Shanghai and the social panic, it is proposed to suggest that the municipal government implement rent reductions to rescue businesses in distress and avert crises. (Reasons) I have observed that the commercial decline and social panic in Shanghai in recent years have been on the verge of collapse, especially this year with the bankruptcy of rural areas and the commercial recession, which has clearly presented an unprecedented phenomenon of depression. Our national product manufacturers are particularly distressed by this adversity. Since the beginning of this year, prices have continued to fall, sales channels have become narrower, resulting in the stagnation of goods and the accumulation of goods like mountains, and huge expenditures that cannot be stopped. It is unpredictable that the current situation will become more and more unfavorable, and the crisis will become more and more obvious. If we do not urgently seek to save it, the demise of Shanghai can be counted on the days, and its impact on the national economy and the people's livelihood is unbearable. I am heartbroken by what I have witnessed, so I do not hesitate to offer my humble suggestions for relief, hoping that you will consider them carefully. Since the "January 28th Incident" in Shanghai, our national vitality has already been greatly damaged. The loss of the four northeastern provinces, the communist bandits in Jiangxi, Fujian and other provinces, the frequent disasters everywhere, and the heavy taxes have led to the daily decline of national products and the increasing dumping of foreign goods, resulting in an uncountable outflow of money. Although enthusiastic people have worked hard to promote and advocate national products, their words have been of no use, and the actual results are zero. Because when looking around, Chinese people all have bad habits of abandoning the old and liking the new, worshipping Europeanization, pursuing external appearances, and disregarding the national foundation, resulting in fruitless efforts and no way to remedy the situation. This is the reason why our national product industry has suffered. In addition, the high rents in Shanghai in recent years have reached their extreme. At a time when people's purchasing power is weak and social finance is in panic, various businesses are in dire straits and have almost no business to speak of, eventually leading to empty doors and few customers. Although they use various methods to attract customers, it is nothing more than competing with their peers. This situation is not unique to all industries in Shanghai, but also to businesses in the interior, and Shanghai businesses are the most distressed. Because rents in Shanghai continue to rise, endlessly, and the burden on various businesses is too heavy, and the income from operations is used to pay the rent, and they are still worried that it is not enough, eventually leading to the inability to operate, and the situation is bound to collapse completely. However, the landlords, in this situation, can they be spared? Looking back at the newly built commercial buildings on various roads, which were quickly rented out in the past and the demand exceeded the supply, are now empty for more than a year and no one cares about them. The crux of the matter is self-evident. It is like this for businesses, and it is like that for landlords, both suffering losses and perishing together. If we do not change our course, will the harm not be severe? I have bones in my throat and dare not remain silent, so I have listed the reasons and put forward the proposal. Whether it is appropriate or not, I am waiting for the public to decide. (Methods) If agreed, please have the Municipal Social Bureau of the Municipal Government order the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to convene the Taxpaying Chinese Association of the Concessions, the General Federation of Citizens of the Special District, and other relevant organizations to form a Rent Evaluation Committee to jointly discuss and decide on methods to persuade Chinese and Western landlords in Shanghai to quickly and voluntarily reduce rents, thereby alleviating business difficulties, maintaining business, and taking care of the livelihood of citizens, and also avoiding the huge losses of newly built commercial buildings remaining empty for a long time. It is truly a case of achieving several benefits with one move.

The detectives, following the instructions, went to the China Garden at the specified address around 3:00 PM the day before yesterday for a secret ambush. One detective disguised himself as a worker, holding a red paper package and standing guard. Around 4:00 PM, two men were seen approaching to make contact. The detectives rushed forward and arrested both men. They were taken to the police station. During the preliminary hearing yesterday morning, one of the men, identified as Tong Lianzhong, 27 years old, from Shaoxing, currently residing on the upper floor of the Hua Fang Laundry at No. 72, Tianzhu Church Street, French Concession, confessed that Tong Baoshun, the deceased owner of Yongli Dyeing Factory, was his uncle, and Xie was his aunt. Because he had been unemployed for a long time and was struggling to make a living, he resorted to extorting his aunt. The two threatening letters were written by his roommate, Liao Hanmin. Today, he, along with Liao and Jin Bingkang, who was arrested at the same time, went to China Garden to collect the money, but were apprehended. Liao had already taken the opportunity to escape. The other man, identified as Jin Bingkang, 19 years old, from Suzhou, residing at No. 10, Fumin Street, Xinbeimen, also confessed without hesitation to conspiring with Tong to send letters to Tong Xie for extortion. As the matter concerned extortion, an official document was prepared to transfer the two suspects to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Xing Zhonghe of Yonghecheng Store Accused of Spreading Rumors and Forging Documents: Cai Renbao, Zhang Zhuping, and Others Sue the First Special Court; Continued Hearing Yesterday with Testimony from Telecommunications Bureau Staff: |The Handwriting on the Telegram Draft is the Same as the Handwriting on Another Document| 166

Xing Zhonghe (also known as Zhonghe), the manager of Yonghecheng Store at No. 529 Tianjin Road, specializes in the raw silk business in Shanghai. There are many stores in Shanghai engaged in the same business, so competition is fierce. Hengsheng Public on Tianjin Road and Yifengchang on Jiangxi Road also operate in this industry. The two stores have business dealings with various stores in Shandong Qingzhou Zhoucun Zhoufang and other places. Suddenly, at the beginning of August this year, they received telegrams from Shanghai stating that Hengsheng Public and Yifengchang owed excessive amounts of money to the bank and had decided to seize their goods, causing stores in other places to mistakenly believe it was true and not send goods to Shanghai for consignment sales. After investigation by Cai Renbao and Zhang Zhuping, the managers of the two stores, it was discovered that the person who sent the telegrams was Xing Zhonghe, the manager of Yonghecheng. Because Xing had previously been the manager of Yuhecheng Silk Store, Yuhecheng owed money to Hengsheng Public and Yifengchang. Cai and others repeatedly demanded payment, leading to a feud. As a means of revenge, Xing took this action. After the matter was clarified, Cai filed a lawsuit with the First Special District Court accusing Xing of spreading rumors and forging documents. The case has been heard several times. Because the court wanted to summon the telegraph bureau's receiving clerk to ask who sent the telegrams and investigate various evidence and witnesses, the hearing was postponed to yesterday afternoon. The receiving clerk on duty at the telegraph bureau on July 31 at 11:00 PM was summoned to court and stated that on that day at 11:00 PM, more than a dozen telegrams were sent to Qingzhou, delivered by a person resembling a tea house waiter. The sender's address was stated to be Wang Shuchang, Baxianfang, Baxian Bridge, French Concession. However, after these telegrams were sent, several were returned because the recipient's address was unknown. When the telegrams were returned to the original sender in Baxianfang, no such person could be found. On August 2, another tea house waiter delivered a telegram to Qingzhou. Because the bureau wanted to inquire about the sender without an address, it tentatively asked this person, who replied that the person who sent the telegrams on July 31 was from Yonghecheng Store on Tianjin Road, and the telephone number was 10075. Therefore, he immediately noted it down for inquiries and returning telegrams. Judge Liu asked, "There are many people who send telegrams every day, how could you ask only this one person?" The clerk replied, "There are many people who send telegrams, but very few who send to Qingzhou. At that time, it was also just a tentative inquiry, because ideally, people from Qingzhou must know the situation of their fellow villagers." At this point, Judge Liu also summoned Xing Shiying, Li Cengxing, and others, witnesses presented by Xing Zhonghe's side, to ask whether they had sent telegrams and who had written them. He also ordered them to write numbers in court for handwriting examination. The lawyers for the plaintiffs, Cai Liucheng and Sun Yuan, stated that the signature on the telegram draft submitted by the telegraph bureau clerk for the telegrams sent on July 31 contained numbers, and it was discovered that there were similarities with the handwriting on another document. They requested the court to pay attention and submitted the document with the same handwriting for review. The court then adjourned the hearing to continue on the 18th of this month.

Xiang Zhejuan, Chief Prosecutor of the First Special Court, Sworn in Yesterday 167

Xiang Zhejuan, the chief prosecutor of the Procuratorate of the Shanghai First Special District Court, arrived in office on September 15. Yesterday, he formally held a swearing-in ceremony. Representatives from various political, military, judicial, and legal circles in the city, as well as the Bar Association, the Municipal Council, and others, attended the ceremony enthusiastically. The details are as follows:

Hall Arrangement 168

The hall was located in the Sixth Civil Tribunal on the third floor of the new building on the east side of the First Special Court. Above the lintel outside the court, a white cloth banner with the words "Hall" was hung. Inside the court, the portrait and will of Sun Yat-sen were placed in the center, with the Party and National flags crossed. Above them was the inscription "The World is for All," and on both sides were the couplets "The Revolution Has Not Yet Succeeded; Comrades Must Continue to Strive." The order of the inauguration ceremony and the oath were also posted on the left and right walls, respectively. The court also had seats for the supervisors, the swearer, Party representatives, guests, and newspaper reporters. The Party and National flags and couplets were also hung high at the entrance of the court. The arrangements were quite grand.

Swearing-in Program 169

(1) Supervisor takes the chair; (2) Swearer takes his place; (3) All stand at attention; (4) Sing the Party anthem; (5) Pay the highest respect to the Party flag, the National flag, and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen; (6) The chairman respectfully reads the will; (7) Silent mourning for three minutes; (8) Swearer takes the oath; (9) Supervisor gives instructions; (10) Party representative delivers a speech; (11) Guests give speeches; (12) Swearer answers; (13) Ceremony concludes; (14) Photograph.

Oath Recorded 170

I solemnly swear that I will strictly abide by the will of the Prime Minister, obey the Party's doctrines, abide by the laws, be loyal to my duties, and work hard in my position. I will never waste a penny or misuse a person, and I will never engage in embezzlement or accept bribes. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment. This is my oath.

Guest List 171

Guests included Wu Tiecheng, Commander of the Songhu Garrison and Mayor of Shanghai, Yu Ming, Director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Office in Shanghai, Shen Jiayi, President of the Second Branch Court of the High Court, Shen Xiqing, President of the Shanghai District Court, Guo Yunguan, President of the First Special Court, Ying Shi, President of the Second Special Court, He Dehui, Manager of the Municipal Council, Chen Tingrui, Executive Director of the Bar Association, Tao Baichuan, Party representative, the presiding judges, judges, prosecutors, and clerks of the civil and criminal tribunals of the First Special Court, and reporters from various newspapers, totaling about two to three hundred people. Wang Zhennan, Chief Prosecutor of the Second Branch Court of the High Court, was specially sent by the Ministry of Justice to supervise the oath.

Excerpts from Speeches 172

At 3:00 PM, the supervisor, the swearer, and all the guests, led by the ushers, stepped into the hall and performed the ceremony. First, the supervisor, Wang Zhennan, delivered a speech, mainly expressing the hope that Chief Prosecutor Xiang would not feel that his work was difficult due to the fact that the prosecutorial powers were bound by various agreements. He should concentrate his efforts and strive hard to live up to the expectations of the government, society, and people. Next, Tao Baichuan, the representative of the Municipal Party Department, delivered a speech, encouraging him to handle cases quickly, without wrongful convictions or leniency, and quoted the words of Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, "Documents are imprisoned for a long time," as a warning. Next, Mayor Wu delivered a speech, stating that although the concessions had various relationships, causing the prosecutorial powers to be subject to considerable restrictions, he hoped that the Chinese people living in the concessions would recognize their status and respect Chinese law, so that the exercise of prosecutorial power, even if slightly restricted, would not be difficult to gradually expand. In addition, the speeches of the guests are temporarily omitted. Finally, Chief Xiang stood up, thanked him, and withdrew.

He was Truly Loyal in Serving Others: |Alas, He Died in Service| 173

Zhang Dexiang, a 58-year-old from Zhenjiang, had been running Yetai Shoe Repair Shop at No. 452 North Henan Road for many years. Zhang was peaceful, amiable, and kind, so the neighbors around him praised him. If friends and relatives had urgent needs, he never refused. He had previously acted as a guarantor for someone, borrowing 500 yuan from his friend Yao. Later, the creditor suddenly disappeared. It was said that he had committed suicide by drowning himself due to economic difficulties. In August of this year, Yao filed a lawsuit with the First Special Court, and the court ruled that Zhang should settle the case with 300 yuan. He was to pay 150 yuan first. Unexpectedly, the night before, when Zhang suddenly went out and had not returned, Yao suddenly arrived and claimed to his wife, Wang, that half of the remaining amount was still owed and had to be returned immediately, otherwise he would seal up the store. After Zhang returned, she truthfully told him what had happened. Zhang, hearing this, felt resentful because the business in the store was not very good and he could not raise the money for a while, so he became weary of the world. He secretly swallowed opium smoke and committed suicide. Later, his wife discovered it and sent him to the hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he died soon after. The hospital reported it to the Hongkou Police Station, which ordered Detective Zhao Lianbi to investigate. After investigation, the body was taken to the Feilun Road Coroner's Office. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Zhang Junqing of the First Special Court, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the office to examine the body. According to the report of the deceased's wife, Zhang Wang, Zhang examined the body and determined that the deceased, Zhang Dexiang, a male, had indeed died of opium poisoning during his lifetime. The body was handed over to his wife, Zhang Wang, who signed a statement to take it back for burial.

A Female Bank Robber: Using a Toy Gun as a Weapon; The Guard Bravely Chases and Captures Him 174

At 12:30 PM yesterday, a middle-aged man suddenly entered the Women's Commercial Bank at No. 392 Nanjing Road. After lingering for a while, he left. Not long after, the man suddenly returned, holding an empty flour bag in one hand and a pistol in the other. He pointed the gun at the chest of Zhao Yuhua, the bank's guard No. 1471, and threatened him. Zhao knew he was a robber, but because the robber had entered alone and had no accomplices, he thought of resisting. He forcibly grabbed the gun pointed at his chest, intending to seize it. Seeing that the gun had been seized, the robber abandoned it and fled out the door. Zhao also chased after him madly. At the intersection of Tianjin Road, Zhao reported the incident to Chinese Detective Lang Zuyin and detective Bao Wang Rulin, who arrived and arrested the man, taking him to the Old Gate Police Station. He confessed that his name was Xu Zhongyuan, a native of Tianjin, who had been doing business in his hometown. Later, he fled to Shanghai after stealing items. Now that he had used up all the money, he thought of a desperate measure. The pistol was not real but a toy purchased from the Sincere Company. The detectives took him into custody. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Criminal Tribunal of the First Special District Court. Ru Baoyi, the police station's lawyer, presented the case and stated that further investigation was needed, requesting an extension of the hearing. The defendant confessed without denying the charges. Presiding Judge Feng Shide reviewed the confession and ordered him to be remanded in custody for further hearing.

Hengfeng Road Oil Press Fire Causes Over Ten Thousand Yuan in Losses 177

Yuanda Oil Press, located at No. 79 Hengfeng Road, Zhabei, with an oil storage facility adjacent to the oil press, was well-equipped. It was established by Li from Haiyan, Zhejiang Province, and others as a joint venture. It had been operating for eleven years, with fairly good business. However, yesterday morning at around 8:00 AM, the motor inside the oil press suddenly short-circuited. Efforts to save it were unsuccessful, and thick smoke quickly filled the area, turning into a raging inferno. The machine room was the first to be destroyed, and the fire spread to the oil storage facility, which contained over two hundred dan of soybean oil. Adding fuel to the fire, the flames burned even more fiercely, reaching the sky and becoming uncontrollable. Nearby residents, young and old, helped each other to move boxes and trunks, fleeing in a hurried panic, causing immediate chaos. Fortunately, the Second Branch of the Fourth District and the Zhabei fire brigades received the alert and arrived promptly. They made every effort to control the situation while bravely fighting the fire. However, the soybean oil had already been heated by the intense flames and was completely ablaze, making water ineffective. Firefighters then tried to contain the fire to prevent it from spreading, while also meticulously battling the blaze. It was not until around 11:00 AM that the fire was extinguished. The oil storage facility was completely destroyed. Fearing reignition, one fire engine was left at the scene to spray water. It returned at around 1:00 PM. After the incident, the total loss to the factory was estimated to be over ten thousand yuan. He Hanhua, the factory accountant (age 27, from Wuxi), was taken to the Second Branch of the Fourth District for questioning after the incident. As the factory owner could not be found, He Hanhua was temporarily detained pending further investigation.

Mother Interferes with Daughter's Right to Correspond, Scolds Her, Daughter Angered and Jumps into River 178

Tang Yunxiang, a 17-year-old girl from Xinghua, came to Shanghai with her mother several years ago. They currently reside at No. 123 Tongxing Lane, Wuzhou Road. She is not yet married. Yunxiang has a cousin named Yu Baolin, who is 19 years old and unmarried. He lives in their hometown of Xinghua. Tang and Yu have had a close relationship since childhood, and their affection deepened as they grew older. They pledged to be together for life. However, Yunxiang kept their relationship a secret from her mother, believing that the time was not yet right. After Yunxiang came to Shanghai with her mother, although they could not see each other every day, they exchanged letters frequently. This shows the depth of their love for each other. However, her mother noticed that Yunxiang was receiving more letters than usual, and became suspicious. She wanted to find out who was writing to her. Yesterday, Yu Baolin sent another letter to Yunxiang, but her mother intercepted it when she was out. She immediately took it to a scholar to decipher the meaning. After reading it, her mother became furious, believing that young women should not engage in love affairs with men. She scolded Yunxiang severely. Feeling hopeless, Yunxiang secretly left the house and walked to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company wharf, where she attempted to drown herself. Fortunately, a patrol boat from the Water Police Department saw her and rescued her. After learning the details, she was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment, and is expected to recover fully.

Features of the Newly Revised Latest Telegraph Code 179

The Telegraph Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications has reprinted the Ming Mi Telegraph Code, originally compiled and printed in 1929, as the previous edition has sold out. The content of this edition has been significantly revised and expanded, including: (1) Enlarged commonly used characters; (2) Added Roman alphabet telegraph codes; (3) Clear radical classification with stroke count annotations; (4) Added Four-Corner Code difficult character lookup table; (5) Added several hundred new characters and removed over forty duplicate characters; (6) Added telegraph code date and time table; (7) Specially prepared secret code page check table; (8) Attached list of names and rates for telegraph offices nationwide; (9) Attached various telegraph service regulations and instructions for sending telegrams, etc. It is comprehensive, neatly bound, and priced very affordably at only two jiao per copy to cover costs. It is an essential book for all sectors and institutions. It is reported that the local International Telegraph Office, Telegraph Office, and various wireless and submarine telegraph receiving and sending offices are selling it, and major bookstores are also acting as agents.

Inspection Reports of Two Banks 180

Central Bank Issue Reserve 178th Inspection Report: This committee, in accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the issuance of convertible banknotes of this bank. The 178th inspection was held on November 10, 1933, at the Issuing Bureau of this bank. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 67,743,468 silver dollars, including 62,157,929 silver dollar notes and 5,585,539 subsidiary currency notes. Total amount of convertible banknote reserve: 67,743,468 silver dollars, including 55,477,468 silver dollars in cash reserve. The cash reserve is stored as follows: 51,600,7915 dollars in the issuing vault of this bank, 2,066,418 dollars in branch offices in various ports, and 1,810,3135 dollars in deposits with other banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 12,266,000 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold unit convertible banknotes issued: 416,715.40 customs gold units. Total amount of customs gold unit convertible banknote reserve: 416,715.40 customs gold units. The reserve includes 6,995.39 taels of standard gold, which is equivalent to 416,715.40 customs gold units at the fixed price of 59,57. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby issued. November 11, 1933. Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Li Fusun, Supervisors Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Ji.

Inspection Report of the Issuance Reserve of the China Reclamation Bank: The issuing vault and the business vault of the China Reclamation Bank have always been completely separated. According to the regulations of the bank's articles of association, the cash reserve should be above 70% and the guarantee reserve should be below 30%. On the 11th of this month, certified public accountant Wang Zikang, together with representatives of the directors and supervisors Xu Ji and Xu Busun, inspected the results as follows: Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 5,342,000 silver dollars. Total amount of convertible banknote reserve: 5,342,000 silver dollars. The cash reserve is 4,170,300 silver dollars, and the guarantee reserve is 1,171,700 silver dollars. The above two items account for approximately 78% of the cash reserve and approximately 22% of the guarantee reserve. This report is hereby issued.
