Tense Sino-Japanese Relations in the International Arena 261

— A recording of Mr. Dong Xian Guang's Speech by Zhu Yu

1. The Inevitability of the Russo-Japanese War: Since September 18th, Japan has advanced and occupied the entirety of Southern Manchuria, thereby sharing a border of thousands of miles with Soviet Russia. Initially, the Japanese were extremely cautious. When Ma Zhanshan's troops held the Nenjiang Bridge, the Japanese repeatedly assured the Soviets that they would not cross the bridge. However, the frenzied Japanese soldiers paid no heed and soon occupied Qiqihar. The Japanese then used their silver tongue to declare that they would not cross the Chinese Eastern Railway. Subsequent events revealed that the Japanese army not only crossed the Chinese Eastern Railway but also drove straight into Manzhouli, forcing Ma Zhanshan and Su Bingwen's troops into Russian territory. By this point, the Japanese saw that Soviet Russia was as docile as a lamb, unable to resist, and their previous cautious and humble attitude, fearing offense, underwent a major transformation. From then on, their ambition grew, and they focused on seizing the Chinese Eastern Railway, rebuilding it to directly connect Korea and Manzhouli, thereby facilitating military transportation.

In addition, three more issues deserve our attention: (1) The Japanese Navy has always dominated the Western Pacific. All important ports are in its hands. When Japan presented China with the Twenty-One Demands, it forbade China from leasing any port to another country as a naval base in the future. The long-term intentions are evident! Now, in the Western Pacific, only the Soviet's Vladivostok is a cause for concern. Once developed, it would be a formidable rival to Japan. Therefore, they must occupy this important base of the Soviet Navy. This alone is enough to be the spark for a future Russo-Japanese War! (2) The Sakhalin Island issue. After the last Russo-Japanese War, the Japanese demanded that Russia cede the island and secretly sent geologists to survey it. The results indicated that the island's oil fields were all in the south, so the Japanese gained the southern part of the island, fully expecting to acquire a treasure trove. Who knew that ten years later, another survey revealed that the oil fields were all in the northern part of the island, which remained in Soviet hands. One can imagine their frustration! This is something that they must obtain, making it worthy of a war. (Note: The oil field theory was mentioned by Admiral Du Xigui to Japanese senior naval officers when he went to Japan to investigate the navy a few years ago, and it is considered credible.) (3) Currently, the border between Soviet Russia and Japan stretches for thousands of miles, and conflicts can occur at any time. The Soviet army can invade Manzhouli at any moment. Therefore, the Japanese are trying to drive them beyond Lake Baikal to develop Southern Manchuria with peace of mind. If these three things cannot be achieved, the three northeastern provinces will never develop. Everyone has the impression of a future Russo-Japanese War. Which capitalist would be willing to invest? With the intensity of modern aerial bombing, a city can be destroyed in five or six days. For the sake of stabilizing people's hearts and promoting the prosperity of Southern Manchuria, the Japanese must fight a war. Otherwise, after making many sacrifices and seizing Manchuria, what benefits would there be?

2. War Preparations on Both Sides: Since the completion of the railway section between Dunhua and Jihui, Manchuria has been able to directly connect with Korea, reducing transportation time by twenty-four hours, greatly improving convenience. In the future, if the Japanese successfully purchase the Chinese Eastern Railway and rebuild it, it will be even more seamless and efficient. However, this is unlikely to happen. The Russians may resolutely refuse. Currently, Japanese officers, especially in the army, tell their soldiers every day that their hypothetical enemy is Soviet Russia, and the army is filled with anti-Russian sentiment, just as the United States is their hypothetical enemy in the navy. Most of the Japanese army is being trained in the northern regions. They train in sub-zero temperatures with very thin clothing, resulting in many deaths and injuries. However, once training is completed, the results will be impressive. Of course, this is also specially prepared against Russia, because the main Russo-Japanese war will undoubtedly be in Siberia and the northern Manchuria area. Japanese Army Minister Araki recently requested the government to issue 100 million yuan in public bonds to manufacture sophisticated military equipment, with special emphasis on chemical warfare, which has made great progress in the past two or three years. One-third of the 100 million yuan is used for this. At the same time, the troops stationed in Manchuria were all placed under the command of the Kwantung Army Headquarters to achieve unified command. On one hand, they recruit and train Japanese, Russians, and Cossacks to prepare for war. Turning to the Soviet side: they are actively manufacturing submarines and destroyers in the Heihe area, with the obvious intention of attacking the Japanese Navy. Recently, the actions of merchant ships in Vladivostok have been monitored to prevent the leakage of secrets, and many forts have been built there, suitable for both offense and defense. The double track of the Siberian Railway has been completed. It is said that the reason for the Russian failure in the last Russo-Japanese War was the slow single-track transportation, so the impact of this is undoubtedly significant. Two and a half months ago, the Soviet Army Chief of Staff personally inspected the Heihe area in the Far East, showing the extreme tension of the situation. Currently, there are between 300 and 500 Soviet military aircraft on the Far Eastern border. The number of troops is unknown, but I estimate that it is around 200,000 to 300,000.

3. When Will the Soviet-Japanese War Break Out? No one can say for sure. It may break out tomorrow. It seems that Japan will always launch the attack first. Soviet Russia will never take the offensive. The Japanese secret document released by the Russian side on the tenth of last month stated: The Japanese government sent personnel to Changchun to secretly instruct the Manchurian authorities to not rush into a challenge against Russia, and it would be best to launch the attack in the spring of 1935. From this, it seems that war may not break out within a year. The day before yesterday, a newspaper reported that eight or nine Japanese military aircraft flew into Soviet Russia to conduct reconnaissance. Such incidents are most likely to cause misunderstandings and conflicts. If the Russian side shoots down one or two with anti-aircraft guns, war may be imminent. At the same time, both sides have intelligence agents in Tokyo and Manchuria conducting secret work. If one or two are arrested and executed, there is a risk of war breaking out. Some say that the war will definitely break out this December or next spring, because winter warfare is most suitable in Siberia, but this is just speculation. In about a month or two, there should be a new development in Russo-Japanese relations, depending on whether the negotiations on the Chinese Eastern Railway continue. At that time, both sides will make their final and greatest decisions!

Activity University 262

— Si Cheng

We, a group of young people, are dropouts driven out by aristocratic schools. When we hold back our tears, clench our fists, and embark on the road of society, it is clear that the pressure of life and the monotony of work gradually deprive us of the opportunity to seek knowledge. However, on the other hand, in our professional lives, we can experience practical life experience. If at the same time we do not give up our spare time for self-study, and we adequately connect our book learning with our practical life experiences, the improvement we make will be far beyond what a "hotel-like" school could provide.

But we have felt that it is very difficult to study alone. People whose willpower is not firm often lose perseverance. Because of various social obstacles and temptations, a young person entering society is most likely to lose their original courage and let themselves decline. This can be said to be the most common phenomenon in our group. Even if one is not tempted by society and can persevere in overcoming difficulties, studying alone is often tedious and insufficient. Of course, progress is very slow. I have discussed these difficulties with many friends, and as a result, we came up with a very good solution. This method has been of great benefit to us to this day, so I dare to write it out and tell every friend who is struggling to study on their own.

This is not a difficult thing. Organize colleagues in your workplace or nearby friends who are studying the same subject into a small group. This small group does not need any funding or procedures, just a weekly meeting. During this meeting, we decide on the various problems that everyone will study in the following week. During this week, each person's self-study should focus on the specified problem (naturally, the specified question)

The problems need to be raised by each person and passed by everyone). The following week, everyone reports on what they have learned. Of course, this cannot be completely consistent. Thus, we can debate based on our own insights and provide the most complete answer to the specified problem (if it cannot be resolved in one meeting, it is moved to the next meeting). At the same time, we decide on the various problems that should be studied next time.

In this way, we can not only gain rapid understanding and progress through debate, but also solve the tediousness and insufficiency of self-study, and make our self-study become systematic learning. At the same time, we can spend a Sunday with nothing to do and benefit greatly. I believe that whether you are studying literature, social science, or natural science, you can use this method appropriately. On the other hand, you can also gain significant benefits in practicing speaking and cultivating team spirit. We can even call it "Our University."

In short, use the spirit of the group to generate the correct power to drive everyone forward, and each person becomes a part of the group, creating this group, making it powerful, and enabling each person to achieve effective self-study and increase the rate of self-study.

I hope that "Our Universities" exist everywhere.

Outlying Postal Agency: Tian Dan's Shrine at the City God Temple 263

— Bai Shi An

Yunnan Pu'er Correspondence

Because farmers in my hometown are suffering from economic oppression and rural bankruptcy, they are gradually changing from small landlords and rich peasants to middle peasants, from middle peasants to small peasants, and from tenant farmers to hired laborers. As for the lives of ordinary farmers, it is simply inhumane. A year of hard work is truly braving the wind and rain, and working under the stars and moon. The working hours can be said to be infinitely long, at least more than twelve hours. With such long working hours, their daily income must be considerable. But the facts tell us the exact opposite. Ordinary farmers grow wheat and cotton, but they mostly eat coarse grains, wear tattered clothes, and live in thatched huts. Except for festivals and special banquets, it is not easy to have meat. Farmers who are slightly more prosperous have at least two meals of porridge a day; the poor do not even have rice for three meals a day. In the event of a famine or unexpected natural or man-made disasters, it is even worse, and they cannot even get enough coarse grain porridge. As a last resort, they have no choice but to borrow at high interest, sell their wives and children, or sell all their plows, cattle, and household implements. If they still cannot survive, then wild fern roots, yams, tree leaves, and garlic are the only food to fill their stomachs. The old and weak cannot even find these, so they can only starve to death. My grandmother often said to me, "The world is not right now. In the past, which family didn't have grain stored in the granary after the autumn harvest? Which family didn't have over a hundred strings of cash to spend for the New Year? Now, most people are 'renting cattle to farm the land, and then encountering natural disasters.' Fifteen or sixteen years ago, the fields in this village and section always belonged to the people who farmed them. Those who could pay the grain tax were so powerful!" Indeed! Eighty percent of the good paddy fields in our village have now gone into the hands of wealthy people in the city.

Schools are important places, but the poor are not allowed to enter. Farmers are born without the opportunity to study, so their knowledge is naturally lacking. Therefore, local bullies and gentry can seize and take from the farmers as they please, running businesses with their surplus loan capital! Farmers must use their houses or farmland as collateral when borrowing money, and the interest rate is five to six percent. If they borrow one dan of grain, they must return two dan when repaying it. When farmers need to use oxen for plowing, they must exchange their labor for the landlord's cattle to plow their own fields. As for the land rented to farmers, the amount of rent paid is approximately half of the total production capacity of the land. In the event of floods, droughts, insect plagues, wind disasters, or epidemics, the harvest is often reduced to 50% or less, or even no harvest at all. In addition, as the number of poor people increases daily, bandits and thieves rise up, so the cultivated land shrinks daily, and no one dares to cultivate it.

The fields of ordinary small landlords and rich peasants suffer a large reduction in annual income because tenants do not dare to cultivate them. Many fields are even left barren and unattended. Plains of tens of acres are still natural wilderness. On the other hand, due to the increasing economic aggression from the outside world, most of the daily necessities are purchased from foreign goods, especially clothing-related goods. This kind of foreign economic aggression naturally has a direct impact on the more affluent small landlords and rich peasants, causing them to suffer great economic losses and gradually become impoverished. As for the heavy taxes, taking only the land tax as an example, the land tax on the same land is now more than thirty times higher than it was thirty years ago, and all kinds of miscellaneous taxes and special taxes are innumerable, such as slaughter tax, live cattle tax, cattle slaughter reporting fees, special education funds, underworld money surcharges, deed tax surcharges, tobacco and alcohol surcharges, grain tax, militia fees, rural cleaning fees, apportionment fees, household registration fees, deed verification tax, weighing tax... and so on. The result of this increased taxation is naturally a fatal blow to the landlords. Due to these various reasons, there is no way for ordinary small landlords to avoid going down the road of bankruptcy. As a result of bankruptcy, small landlords naturally cannot afford the land tax and miscellaneous taxes, and no one dares to cultivate the land. Even if they cultivate it themselves, the value of the harvest is not enough to offset the loss of land tax and taxes due to natural and man-made disasters. Undoubtedly, ordinary people do not dare to buy this large amount of land either. Because small landlords and rich peasants cannot get any benefit anyway, in order to avoid the extortion and persecution of corrupt officials, they have no choice but to cut it off with pain. People often send Tian Dan to the City God Temple and hang him on the Buddha cabinet of the City God. Therefore, the land in my hometown has gradually become the property owned by the City God.

This is not lamenting the decline, but just a page of the reality of decline.

Amateur Cafe

"Thrift and Savings" vs. "Timely Purchases" 264

— Zhang Yong

"Thrift and savings" is naturally a treasure worth telling your younger brother and father telling his son. Especially for us young fellows under the wings of our employers, we should regard it as the "golden rule," because our employers often stroke the sparse short stubble on their chins and say to us very proudly: "When I was as old as you, I didn't earn as much salary as you do now, but I squeezed out a fraction of my monthly salary and saved it. Later, it accumulated more and more, so I partnered with others to open a shop, gradually developed, and opened my own shop, and then opened several shops alone. If you can be as thrifty and saving as I am, I guarantee that you will have a bigger business than I did before you reach my age."

On the reverse side of "thrift and savings" is "timely purchases." If "thrift and savings" is generally recognized as the secret to wealth, then "timely purchases" is, needless to say, undoubtedly a recipe for "not having food to eat." But I heard that the "recession" of the American empire was caused by the people's unwillingness to make "timely purchases." Originally, producers work hard to produce, relying on someone to consume. If producers produce a large number of products, but consumers do not make "timely purchases," then producers will have to reduce or stop production due to the stagnation of capital and the accumulation of goods. Under these actions of reducing and stopping production, there is no doubt that many employees of production enterprises will lose part or all of their purchasing power. Thus, the products produced by the producers will naturally suffer an even greater blow. Under this recession situation, the American empire saw the novel spectacle of President Hoover advising the people to make "timely purchases." It is said that if every citizen of the American empire could spend all the money they have in the bank and the wages they earn every week without hesitation to buy things, then in the near future, the American empire could see the prosperity of 1929 again, and every citizen would no longer experience the panic of bread.

"Thrift and savings" is a great principle, and "timely purchases" also sounds logical. Everyone has their own reasons. Although these two hats are not the same size, they are equally comfortable when worn on the head. What kind of logic is this in economics? It is really a bit incomprehensible. Now let's put aside the logic of economics and study whether the path of "thrift and savings" or the path of "timely purchases" is wider and easier to walk in China, a backward and semi-colonial country.

In this backward production, semi-colonial country whose entire economic organization is dominated by imperialism, it is naturally impossible to talk about any economic policy that can save the current economic crisis. In today's year of global recession, there is no need for China to be polite, and it is inevitable to come up with a set of "sluggish sales" tricks. In the United States, perhaps "timely purchases" can activate the funds of various enterprises. If we also follow suit and play this game, and recklessly make "timely purchases," wouldn't that still result in turning the people's savings in savings banks into boxes and boxes of silver dollars and shipping them overseas? If we yellow-faced Chinese also learned from the Americans and spent the only five cents in our pockets to buy a glass of beer, then people would not need to make "timely purchases" anyway. They only need to dump all the unsold goods on this Far Eastern market, and they would not be afraid of easily saving the recession and returning to prosperity.

Therefore, the American empire advocates "timely purchases" to save the crisis. If China advocates "timely purchases," it is tantamount to cutting off its own flesh to feed the tiger. People would "swallow it whole without the slightest politeness."

Since the path of "timely purchases" is impassable, then let's take the path of "thrift and savings." Although in this period of social system turbulence and transformation, we dare not dream of becoming "small capitalists" through "thrift and savings," and becoming "big capitalists" from "small capitalists," but society is so chaotic and unorganized, human relationships are so cold, and the world economy has collapsed to such an extent that the demon of unemployment is baring its fangs and claws and preparing to break everyone's lifeline. Isn't "thrift and savings" a "storing grain against famine" plan among our limited passive methods?

Therefore, in the United States, it is really qualified to shout the slogan of "timely purchases" to save the economy of the entire American empire. But in this semi-colonial country whose economic organization is completely dominated by imperialism, I think it is more appropriate to take "thrift and savings" with the individual as the starting point as the slogan.

Amateur Sports

Shuttlecock 265

— Xiao Zheng

(1) Benefits of Kicking Shuttlecock

Kicking shuttlecock is almost a full-body exercise, involving the head, neck, waist, legs, and feet. Practicing in the late autumn and early winter weather is especially suitable. If you can persevere and practice for tens of minutes every morning, in addition to being able to temporarily resist the cold, practicing for a few months will guarantee that your body parts will have unexpected development, which is no less than practicing Baduanjin.

(2) Shuttlecock Manufacturing

It is no longer possible to verify when the shuttlecock was invented. The raw materials for manufacturing a shuttlecock are a piece of soft leather, a duck feather tube, a few chicken feathers, and a large copper coin. First, cut the soft leather into two circular pieces the size of a copper coin, sandwich the copper coin in the middle, and sew along the edges. Then, cut one end of the duck feather tube into a three-pronged shape, sew it in the center of the soft leather, and insert the chicken feathers. Leather shoe stores on the market often sell this kind of shuttlecock, with prices ranging from about four to eight copper coins.

(3) Shuttlecock Kicking Skills and Names

Shuttlecock kicking skills are divided into two categories: "Eight Bigs" and "Eight Smalls." "Eight Bigs" means kicking with one foot while the other foot is also off the ground. "Eight Smalls" also means kicking with one foot while the other foot does not leave the ground. I only know the sounds of the following names, so I will write them out using characters with similar sounds and meanings. If there are any mistakes, please readers correct me.

"Eight Bigs"

(1) Guàn (Guàn is the easiest of the eight bigs. It involves using one foot behind the other to kick the shuttlecock high, and both feet must leave the ground at the same time.)

(2) Guì (Bend one leg into a kneeling position in the crook of the other leg and kick the shuttlecock high.) (Note: Do not kick with the bent leg.)

(3) Yì (Place the sole of one foot on the other leg’s crook and kick the shuttlecock high) (Note: same as above)

(4) Zé (Stack both feet forward and use the foot below to kick the shuttlecock high.)

(5) Piě (Kick the shuttlecock over one leg, then use the other leg to kick the shuttlecock high.) (Note: Kick the shuttlecock high in front of the body, not beside it.)

(6) Guòmén Guàn (Cross the shuttlecock over one leg, action is the same as Guàn)

(7) Guòmén Guì (Cross the shuttlecock over one leg, action is the same as Guì)

(8) Guòmén Yì (Cross the shuttlecock over one leg, action is the same as Yì)

The first four consecutive movements are called "Four Great Kings"; eight consecutive movements are called "Eight Great Heavenly Kings"; the last three consecutive movements are called "Three Crossing the Door"; Guàn
